The Impaler | Description | The Impaler is a keystone passive skill. Whenever a hit from you or your skills impales a target, that hit also impales all nearby enemies, and applies an additional 5 impale debuffs to each (for a total of 6). It then causes each affected enemy to avoid impale for 5 seconds, during which impales cannot be Called from them with Call of Steel.
The Impaler | Mechanics | The Impaler causes hits to inflict 5 additional impale debuffs, for a total of 6, to all enemies in an area, with the downside of preventing the application of more impale debuffs to those enemies for 5 seconds. This can be useful in combination with slow but powerful impaling hits, or potentially in a scenario with low available impale chance.
The Impaler | Mechanics | Impales can be applied when an enemy is killed in one hit, [1] though those impales cannot be Called with Call of Steel until 5 seconds have passed.
The Impaler | Mechanics | Due to its ability to inflict multiple impales with one hit, the Impaler can stack impales on enemies beyond typical methods. For example, by impaling an enemy, waiting for 5 seconds, then impaling them again, an enemy can be left with 6 debuffs that have 5 hits remaining, and 6 debuffs that have 4 hits remaining, for a total of 12. (Or even more through impale duration or Temporal Chains.) While likely impractical, it may become meaningful in combination with for each Impale on Enemy modifiers.
The Impaler | Mechanics | When impaling a non-impaled enemy, the 5 additional impales still count as Impales you inflict on non-Impaled Enemies.
The Impaler | Mechanics | Because the impaler's effect on enemies causes them to avoid impales from all sources, The Impaler may conflict with impaling party members or minions.
The Impaler | Damage calculations | All calculations assume 100% impale chance to make them simple. For characters using impale damage, The impaler keystone has the potential to raise or lower the total damage done. Whether or not the impaler can raise or lower the total damage is dependent on the following factors:
The Impaler | Damage calculations | This example will try to use all of these factors to their highest potential to show that The Impaler does higher damage for certain specific builds.
The Impaler | Location | The Impaler is located on the south side of the tree, on the left side of outer part of the Duelist's area across Crimson Dance.

The Traitor (keystone passive) | Description | The Traitor is a keystone passive skill which gives 4 Flask Charges every 5 seconds for each Flask Slot that is empty. It is only granted by the Brutal Restraint timeless jewel. (The variant with modifier Denoted service of (500–8000) dekhara in the akhara of Balbala mod only.)
The Traitor (keystone passive) | Description | Note that these charges are not split up between the remaining flasks, and instead apply to each one. For example, if there are two empty flask slots and three full ones, each one of the three flasks will gain 8 flask charges, for a total of 24 charges gained every 5 seconds.
The Traitor (keystone passive) | Mechanics | Each equipped flask gains 0.8 charges per second per empty flask slot.
The Traitor (keystone passive) | Location | This keystone will replace (in-game wording " conquer ") any keystones within the radius of the aforementioned variant of Brutal Restraint.
The Unseen Hand | Description | The Unseen Hand is a notable Bloodline Ascendancy passive skill from the Nameless Bloodline that grants an additional ring slot.
The Unseen Hand | Mechanics | Rings equipped the additional ring slot granted by this passive is not considered to be on the left or right ring slot and it does not have a corresponding opposite ring slot. This causes conditional effects that care about whether the ring is in the left or right slot (e.g. Dusk Ring , Snakepit ) or checks for the ring on the opposite slot (e.g. Mark of the Shaper , Kalandra's Touch ) to never activate their effects. Additionally, rings that check for the opposite ring slot will never check this additional ring slot (e.g. Kalandra's Touch will not reflect the third ring's effects).
The Unseen Hand | Mechanics | However, effects that count the number of certain types of items (e.g. Shadowstitch ) or care if all equipped items are a certain type of item (e.g. The Eternity Shroud ) do care about the item in this additional slot.
The Vivid Cat | Description | The Vivid Cat is a notable Bloodline Ascendancy passive skill from the Oshabi Bloodline that causes Elusive to grant increased Mark effect and adds a chance for Elusive to be prematurely removed when it reaches 100% effect.
The Wild Bear | Description | The Wild Bear is a notable Bloodline Ascendancy passive skill from the Oshabi Bloodline that grants maximum rage. In addition, when the user reaches maximum rage, all stacks of rage is removed to grant the Wild Savagery buff , with its duration depending on the amount of rage lost this way.

Timeless Conflict | Description | Timeless Conflict is an Atlas passive skill and Atlas keystone , specifically for the Legion league encounter.
Timeless Conflict | Mechanics | Timeless Conflict disables the Legion timer after interacting with the Legion Monoliths in a map. Instead, breaking out monsters and chests from stasis will contribute progress towards a Schism, shown by a progress bar. Once the progress bar is full, the Schism will occur and the Legion encounter will begin. Breaking out monsters and chests with rewards or more powerful monsters will contribute more progress towards the Schism. [1]
Timeless Conflict | Location | As of version 3.22.0 it is located near the bottom-right of the Atlas passive skill tree inside the Legion cluster containing Protracted Battle and Chain of Command.
Tireless | Description | Tireless is a notable passive skill that grants increased maximum life and reduced cost of skills.
Tireless | Mechanics | This notable passive skill and the three smaller passive nodes leading to it are currently the only sources of generic reduced cost of skills in the game and grant a total of 15%. Besides reducing the mana and life cost of skills, it also reduces the rage cost of skills while using the Chainbreaker Keystone provided by a Lethal Pride Timeless Jewel with the modifier Commanded leadership over (10000–18000) warriors under Akoya.
Tireless | Mechanics | It is additive with other sources of non-generic reduced cost modifiers such as the notable passive skills Righteous Decree and Cannibalistic Rite , as well as the Inspiration Support.
Tireless | Mechanics | Reduced Cost of skills has no effect on the amount of life/mana reserved from skill like Hatred or the soul cost of vaal skills such as Vaal Molten Shell. It however reduces the cost of auras , if those are supported by Divine Blessing Support.

Transcendence | Description | Transcendence is a keystone passive skill that causes armour to grant damage reduction against elemental damage instead of physical damage. It also lowers maximum elemental resistances. [1]
Transcendence | Mechanics | Armour applies to Fire, Cold and Lightning Damage taken from Hits instead of Physical Damage causes armour to defend against elemental damage instead of physical damage. Other armour behaviour is unchanged: it only grants damage reduction against hits , and is normally capped to 90%. Modifiers that cause a percentage of armour to defend against elemental hits (e.g. #% of Armour applies to Fire, Cold and Lightning Damage taken from Hits ) are redundant. [2]
Transcendence | Mechanics | Elemental resistances still mitigate elemental hits, and do so before armour's damage reduction is calculated. Additionally, hits that deal more than one element will have each element individually reduced (rather than the sum of all relevant elements) by the armour value. [3]
Transcendence | Interactions | Because the player can no longer defend against physical damage with armour, items that cause physical damage to be taken as elemental damage (e.g. Cloak of Flame Lightning Coil Dawnbreaker ) can be used to mitigate physical damage instead. It is also possible to obtain non-armour sources of physical damage reduction (e.g. endurance charges , Strength of Blood ).
Transcendence | Interactions | Items like Loreweave or Replica Loreweave can be used to ignore Transcendence's maximum resistance penalty, as well as similar penalties found on e.g. Eternal Damnation.
Transcendence | Interactions | The Fourth Vow 's Armour also applies to Chaos Damage taken from Hits is not prevented by Transcendence; the combination can make armour defend against both elemental and chaos hits.
Transcendence | Location | This keystone will conquer any keystones within the radius of a Militant Faith jewel with modifier Carved to glorify (2000-10000) new faithful converted by High Templar Maxarius.
Transcendence | Related unique items | These unique items (other than Militant Faith ) have the Transcendence modifier, which provides the same effect as this keystone. Taking the keystone in addition to equipping one of these items will impart no additional benefit.

Twist of Fate | Description | Twist of Fate is an atlas passive skill and Atlas keystone that causes any Corrupted Rare maps used in affected Map Devices and any Map crafting options applying to them to be modified unpredictably when opened, with Maps modified in this way having 1-3 additional random Map Modifiers.
Twist of Fate | Mechanics | The resulting map can be any valid map of the same tier based on the player's current Atlas of Worlds modified by socketed Voidstones. If there are no valid maps on the player's current Atlas, it will result in a random map of the same natural tier. Corrupted Tier 17 maps reroll into a random Tier 17 map. Shaper Guardian maps will be rerolled into random T16 maps.
Twist of Fate | Mechanics | Implicit Map Modifiers are not modified, meaning that guaranteed encounter implicits (e.g. from Kirac 's vendor shop or Shadow Shaping ), Elder Guardian / Conquerors maps, or Vaal Temple Map 's " Area contains 10 additional guarded Vaal Vessels " modifiers can be guaranteed regardless of the new map base. Delirium Layers and Enchantments are also retained.
Twist of Fate | Mechanics | The number of explicit modifiers and the specific modifiers on the original map are not retained and is randomly rerolled, as if a Chaos Orb then a Vaal Orb had been applied. This also includes fractured modifiers. The map can randomly roll 4-6 or 8 base modifiers, plus an additional 1-3 modifiers. All of these modifiers are affected by map modifier effect.
Twist of Fate | Mechanics | Map crafting options will still consume one stored free use or require their crafting cost (e.g. X Chaos Orbs ) prior to the randomization.
Twist of Fate | Mechanics | Map fragments (including scarabs ) are not randomized with this keystone.
Twist of Fate | Mechanics | Any quality effects on the map (e.g. from Cartographer's Chisel or Maven's Chisels ) are removed.
Twist of Fate | Mechanics | Twist of Fate can also randomize corrupted blighted maps and blight-ravaged maps , which may be useful to salvage these types of maps with bad modifiers like Monsters cannot be Stunned or Monsters' Action Speed cannot be modified to below base value. It will not change the map's oil anointments.
Twist of Fate | Location | Twist of Fate is located at the center left of the atlas passive skill tree, near the "Delirium" wheel.
Two-Hearted Hunt | Description | Two-Hearted Hunt is an atlas passive skill.
Two-Hearted Hunt | Mechanics | Einhar encounters in maps have a chance of captured red beasts gaining a modifier that provides them a chance of not being consumed when beastcrafting , ranging from 10% to 40% in 10% increments. Red beasts in maps also have an additional Bestiary modifier.

Unending Nightmare | Description | Unending Nightmare is an Atlas passive skill and Atlas keystone , specifically for the Delirium league encounter.
Unending Nightmare | Mechanics | Unending Nightmare causes Delirium fog from the Delirium Mirror to never dissipate in your maps, preventing it from being ended by any method, including by clicking the hotkey or button, meaning that the Delirium fog will add a permanent difficulty modifier to the map it spawns in. The player can claim the Delirium rewards upon its respective reward filling up, dropping on the floor as soon as a bar is filled up a tier, similar to a Delirium Orb map. Also, taking this notable disables the ability to find Simulacrum Splinter s and Delirium Orbs as loot in your maps, either from claiming the Delirium rewards or from killing delirious monsters.
Unending Nightmare | Mechanics | Unending Nightmare also doubles the inherent difficulty scaling that applies based on distance from the Delirium Mirror.
Unending Nightmare | Mechanics | Notably, Delirium rewards will almost always drop at least one Cluster Jewel upon reaching a new reward tier, making it useful especially in SSF.
Unending Nightmare | Location | As of version 3.22.0, it is located near the center-left of the Atlas passive skill tree inside the Delirium cluster containing The Singular Eternity and Descent Into Madness.

Unlight Silhouette | Description | Unlight Silhouette is a notable Bloodline Ascendancy passive skill from the Nameless Bloodline that adds a base life cost to skills equal to its mana cost, but grants added chaos damage based on life spent.
Unlight Silhouette | Mechanics | Skills gain a Base Life Cost equal to 100% of Base Mana Cost : Skills gain a life cost based on the skill's base mana cost before any modifiers apply. Life cost is increased by modifiers to generic or life cost, but not mana cost.
Unlight Silhouette | Mechanics | Skills gain Added Chaos Damage equal to 20% of Life Cost. : This effect works similarly to Archmage Support prior to its rework in version 3.24.0 , though it adds chaos damage instead of lightning damage, and scales based on life cost, not mana cost.
Unlight Silhouette | Mechanics | .if Life Cost is not higher than the maximum you could spend : If the life cost of the skill exceeds the maximum resource pool (typically just unreserved life), all of the added damage from the previous part of the line is nullified. This can be a result of conditional or rotating cost modifiers such as Indigon increasing the cost after the skill is used.
Unlight Silhouette | Mechanics | Cost scaling - The added chaos damage scales with the supported skill's life cost. There are multiple factors or stats that can increase a skill's life cost:
Unlight Silhouette | Mechanics | Note that sacrificing or losing life (e.g. Sacrifice Support , Dark Pact , Rathpith Globe , Chaos Mastery Lose 10% of Life and Energy Shield when you use a Chaos Skill ) do not count as costs.
Unlight Silhouette | Indigon | Indigon is the most efficient method to raise the life cost to its highest functioning percent (100% of unreserved life), with the downside of the damage being nullified once cost exceeds 100% of unreserved life. Indigon can be made more stable by reducing variance in attack or cast speed. Note that mana still needs to be spent to ramp up Indigon; this means that it cannot be used with Blood Magic (the keystone) or Lifetap Support on the ramping skill(s) as these remove the mana cost of the skill.
Unlight Silhouette | Indigon | In addition, due to the rapid spending of life, it will be incredibly difficult to use life as a defensive layer normally. In this case, Dissolution of the Flesh has notable synergy, allowing life to be spent and recovered rapidly (with Module Error: Too many passives found with q_where = passive_skills.name="Eternal Youth" ) without impacting your actual effective health.

Unwavering Stance | Description | Unwavering Stance is a keystone passive skill that grants guaranteed stun avoidance, but prevents the character from evading attacks.
Unwavering Stance | Mechanics | Unwavering Stance sets chance to avoid being stunned to 100% and sets evasion chance to 0%, which means enemies will always hit regardless of their accuracy rating or chance to hit.
Unwavering Stance | Mechanics | Unwavering Stance does not modify evasion rating. This is significant mainly because of the Iron Reflexes keystone, which converts evasion rating to armour. It is therefore possible to utilize the effects of both keystones simultaneously. ( Ghost Dance is also technically not affected.)
Unwavering Stance | Location | Unwavering Stance is located on the bottom left side of the tree, on the intersection between the Marauder, Duelist, and Scion paths.

Unwavering Vision | Mechanics | This keystone disables scarab drops and prevents the use of map fragments (other than Divine Vessel ) and scarabs in your map device alongside a map to enhance it, in exchange for extra points for the Atlas Passive Tree.
Unwavering Vision | Mechanics | It does not prevent the opening of bosses or encounters that exclusively require map fragments such as the Shaper or any Uber pinnacle boss.
Unwavering Vision | Mechanics | It does prevent the use of a Hivebrain Gland.

Vaal Oligarchs | Description | Vaal Oligarchs is an atlas passive skill.
Vaal Oligarchs | Mechanics | Vaal Flesh Merchant is a unique vaal wraith that always spawns inside of temporal incursion encounters when this atlas passive is allocated.
Vaal Pact | Description | Vaal Pact is a keystone passive skill that grants instant life leech to melee attacks, but prevents all other forms of life recovery.
Vaal Pact | Mechanics | Vaal Pact does not affect any other types of leech, such as energy leech or mana leech, as it applies exclusively to life leech. It also has no interactions with Ghost Reaver.
Vaal Pact | Mechanics | While only melee attacks gain instant leech from Vaal Pact, life leech from non-melee sources will function normally. By using Brutal Fervour and a skill that has both a melee and non-melee damage component (e.g. Molten Strike ), you can benefit from both instant leech and overleech.
Vaal Pact | Mechanics | The Cannot Recover Life other than from Leech modifier prevents life recovery from sources that aren't leech or Temporal Rift. This is checked when the player's life is modified; it does not remove life recovery stats from the character entirely. Accordingly, life recovery modifiers can still be used for other purposes through mechanics like Zealot's Oath , Pious Path , or Kaom's Spirit.
Vaal Pact | Location | Vaal Pact is located on the middle layer of the south side, on the east side of the Duelist's area.
Valley of Darkness | Description | Valley of Darkness was an atlas keystone passive skill.
Valley of Darkness | Mechanics | Adds a random Archnemesis modifier to all rare monsters in maps. This increases the difficulty of rare monster encounters (particularly ones with other buffs like Essences or Bestiary Red Beasts), but makes it easier to stack stolen modifiers for things like Headhunter and Inspired Learning.
Valley of Darkness | Location | During version 3.18.0 it was located at the center right of the atlas passive skill tree, near the "Expedition" wheel.

Veteran's Awareness | Strategies | Veteran's Awareness provides significant improvement to physical and elemental defences while a guard skill is up, but provides a significant debuff after a guard skill is lost either by reaching its duration or exhausting its absorption. Proper usage of this keystone requires maximizing the duration and minimizing the downtime/ cooldown of guard skills.

Wandering Path | Description | Wandering Path was an atlas passive skill and Atlas keystone.
Wandering Path | Mechanics | Disables the effects of all notable skills, but doubles the effect of all small passive skills (including travel nodes). The most popular use of this keystone is to stack Adjacent Map Drop Chance, Map Drop Duplication, Item Quantity, and Map Modifier Effect nodes in early mapping to fill out Atlas completion and to boss rush maps with Exarch or Eater influence to farm Invitations. Players can also stack chance to get Master Missions upon map completion, item rarity for map bosses, and Eater/Exarch pack size for Eldritch currency farming, making it incredibly strong for SSF.
Wandering Path | Ruthless mode | In Ruthless mode , instead of granting increased effect to small nodes, it grants 20 Atlas passive skill points.

Wicked Ward | Description | Wicked Ward is a keystone passive skill that prevents energy shield recharge from being interrupted by damage if energy shield recharge began recently , but reduces your base energy shield recharge rate from 33% to 20%.
Wicked Ward | Mechanics | Once energy shield recharge starts, either by not taking damage for a duration (2 seconds by default) or by effects that trigger energy shield recharge such as Xirgil's Crank or Spellbreaker , recharge will not be interrupted by damage for 4 seconds. This effect persists for the full 4 seconds even if energy shield reaches full.
Wicked Ward | Location | Wicked Ward is located on the right side of the upper part of the tree, near the energy shield wheel for the Witch.
Wicked Ward | Related unique items | These unique items have the Wicked Ward modifier, which provides the same effect as this keystone. Taking the keystone in addition to equipping one of these items will impart no additional benefit.

You're the crazy one! | Description | You're the crazy one! is a notable Bloodline Ascendancy passive skill from the Delirious Bloodline that grants the Embrace Madness skill. While active, enemies near your character receive a stack of the Mania debuff every second, but you will be affected by stacking Glorious Madness debuffs.
You're the crazy one! | Mechanics | Mania : Mania applies 4% increased Damage taken, 2% reduced Action Speed and 10% reduced Life and Energy Shield Recovery Rate for 15 seconds and can be inflicted up to 15 times
You're the crazy one! | Mechanics | Mania applies in a radius of 6 metres.
You're the crazy one! | Mechanics | Taking this passive skill also causes random Insanity effects to occur, which are harmless but ominous chat messages or animations.
Zealot | Description | Zealot is a notable passive skill added by the Militant Faith jewel. It requires the listed amount of Devotion to be allocated to function.
Zealot's Oath | Description | Zealot's Oath is a keystone passive skill that applies life regeneration to energy shield instead of life.
Zealot's Oath | Mechanics | Percentage and flat life regeneration becomes percentage and flat ES regeneration. Percentage ES regeneration is based on maximum ES. [1] Percentage based life regeneration can be gained from several unique items and passive skills. ES regen gained this way will only be scaled by ES Recovery Rate, not Life Recovery Rate [2] Life Regeneration Rate modifiers also do not apply.
Zealot's Oath | Mechanics | This will not cause life flasks to recover ES as they give life recovery. [3]
Zealot's Oath | Mechanics | Zealot's Oath causes the user to no longer have life regen, which causes effects that interact specifically with life regeneration amount, such as Pious Path and Kaom's Spirit , to not work with Zealot's Oath. [4]
Zealot's Oath | Location | Zealot's Oath is a standalone keystone located in the northwest side of the tree, close to the Templar 's area.
Zealot's Oath | Related unique items | The following unique items are related to Zealot's Oath:
